	<!-- DFP -->
	
				<div class="js-change-top-ads" 
				data-start-date="2017-10-06" data-start-time="00:00" 
				data-end-date="2017-10-06" data-end-time="23:59" 
				data-new-ads="970x250" data-old-ads="1260x70">
			</div>
<!--/-->
	<!-- Script para alteração de advertising do topo - Formatos: ad-970x250 / ad-1260x70 -->
<script>
	Array.prototype.slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('.js-change-top-ads')).forEach( function(ads) {
		var dateTime = new Date();
		var currentDate = dateTime.getFullYear() + '-'+ (dateTime.getMonth()+1) + '-' + dateTime.getDate();
		var currentTime = dateTime.getHours() + ':' + dateTime.getMinutes() + ':' + dateTime.getSeconds();
		var currentDateTime = Date.parse(currentDate + ' ' + currentTime);
		
		var startDt = ads.getAttribute('data-start-date');
		var startTm = ads.getAttribute('data-start-time');
		var endDt = ads.getAttribute('data-end-date');
		var endTm = ads.getAttribute('data-end-time');
		var nAds = ads.getAttribute('data-new-ads');
		var oAds = ads.getAttribute('data-old-ads');
		var startAds = Date.parse(startDt + ' ' + startTm);
		var endAds = Date.parse(endDt + ' ' + endTm);

		var newAds = document.querySelector('.ad-' + nAds);
		var oldAds = document.querySelector('.ad-' + oAds);

		if (currentDateTime > startAds && currentDateTime <= endAds) {
			newAds.className = 'advertising ad-' + nAds;
			var parentOldAds = oldAds.parentNode;
			parentOldAds.removeChild(oldAds);
			return;
		}
	});

	var ads1260x70 = document.querySelector('.ad-1260x70');

	if (ads1260x70) {
		ads1260x70.className = 'advertising ad-1260x70';
		var parentNewAds = document.querySelector('.ad-970x250').parentNode;
		parentNewAds.removeChild(document.querySelector('.ad-970x250'));
	}

	var adsBtnClose = document.querySelectorAll('.js-ads-button-close');

	if (adsBtnClose) {
		var adsBtClose = Array.prototype.slice.call(adsBtnClose);

		adsBtClose.forEach( function(btn) {
			btn.addEventListener('click', hideAdvertising, false);
		});

		function hideAdvertising(event) {
			var id = event.target.nextElementSibling.id.replace('-area', '');

			event.target.parentNode.style.height = '0px';

			var ad = document.getElementById(id + '-area');
			var parentAd = ad.parentNode;
			parentAd.removeChild(ad);

			var elAd = document.querySelector('.ad-970x250');
			var parentElAd = elAd.parentNode;
			parentElAd.removeChild(elAd);
		}
	}
</script>
<!-- /Script para alteração de advertising do topo - Formatos: ad-970x250 / ad-1260x70 -->

				window._sf_endpt=(new Date()).getTime();
				var e = document.createElement('script');
